## Mac serial lookup

Finding Your Serial [click here](https://www.applefixpros.com/mac-part/)
X
##  If Your Mac Turns On 
If your Mac is working properly, finding the serial number is easy. Just click the Apple menu icon at the top of the screen and select “About This Mac”. You’ll see the serial number displayed along with your Mac’s model number, hardware specifications, and the version of macOS you have installed
## If Your Mac Won’t Turn On
Your Mac’s serial number is printed somewhere on the Mac itself, so you’ll be able to find it if you can’t turn your Mac on. Flip over a MacBook and you’ll see the serial number and model number printed on the Mac itself, near the “Designed by Apple in California” text. On a Mac Mini, you’ll find the serial number on the bottom. On the Mac Pro, you’ll find it on the back panel.

## Mac **Repair**
  * #### Fill Out the Repair Form
Start by completing our Mac Repair Request Form. Once submitted, you’ll receive an email or text message with your prepaid shipping label and detailed packing instructions. We’ll guide you on how to safely ship your MacBook to our repair center — it’s quick and fully insured.
  * #### Send In Your MacBook
Pack your MacBook securely and attach the provided shipping label. Drop it off at the nearest carrier location — shipping is free both ways for most repairs. We’ll notify you as soon as your MacBook arrives and begin the diagnostic process.
  * #### Approve the Quote & Get It Fixed
After inspection, our certified technicians will contact you with a detailed repair quote. Approve it, and we’ll get your MacBook repaired and shipped back to you — fast, professional, and hassle-free.


### Why Choose Apple Fix Pros? 
  * **Same-Day Repairs** – No appointments, no attitude, no lines — just fast, reliable service when you need it
  * **100% Genuine Parts** – Only authentic Apple components, no knock-offs.
  * **1-Year Warranty** – Full coverage for your peace of mind.
  * **Zero Fees Upfront** – Free diagnostics, free estimates, no surprises.

## Commonly asked **questions**
1. If you are local
You can simply call us for a quotation or check our Mac parts page for details and prices about parts.  
No need to ship your Mac — walk in and get it sorted quickly!
2. What is the process?
Simply fill out our repair request form, ship your MacBook using the prepaid label we provide, and wait  
for our team to inspect it. Once inspected, we’ll send you a detailed repair quote for approval before we  
start any work.
3. How do I pay?
Payment is easy and secure. You can pay via credit/debit card, PayPal, or Apple Pay once you  
approve the repair quote. No payment is taken before your approval.
4. How long will this take?
Most repairs are completed same-day or within 1–3 business days after we receive your device,  
depending on the complexity. Shipping times vary based on your location.
5. Are there hidden fees / will you charge me for the repairs without me confirming them?
Never. You are only charged for the repairs you approve. We provide transparent pricing and free  
estimates before starting any work.
6. How will you contact me?
We will contact you via the email or phone number you provide in the repair request form. All updates,  
quotes, and confirmations are sent directly to you.
7. How long do I have to pay?
You have up to 7 days to approve and pay the repair quote. If you need more time, simply contact us  
and we can extend the window.
8. What happens if you can’t fix my device?
We fix 99.9% of Mac issues. If we cannot repair your Mac, we’ll return it to you at no cost. You won’t be  
charged for diagnostics or any unsuccessful repair attempts
9. What happens if I send an item for repair that is not listed on your service offerings?
We’ll contact you immediately to discuss options. If it’s something we cannot service, we will return the  
item safely with no charges.
### Data Responsibility  Disclaimer 
We understand that your data is valuable to you. Data loss during service is always a possibility, and in some cases, data may be unrecoverable, erased, or reformatted during service. For this reason, it is your responsibility to back up all existing data, software, and programs from your product, and to decide whether to erase any such data from your product prior to receiving service.
Apple Fix Pros is not responsible for loss, recovery, or compromise of data, software, programs, or loss of use of your product or other equipment arising out of the services provided. We cannot guarantee that you will get your data back or that you will not lose your data. It is up to you to back up your device.

## Trade In Your Device
Trade in your device, unlock value, and help create a more sustainable future by giving it a new life!
1
####  Fill Out the Form 
Start by completing our quick Sell Your Mac form. Once submitted, you’ll receive an email or text with your prepaid shipping label and simple instructions. Please note — the offer you see on our website is an estimate (a price range). The final offer depends on your Mac’s year, model, condition, and authenticity after inspection. 
2
####  Send In Your Mac 
Pack your Mac securely and ship it using the free prepaid label we send you. There’s no cost to you, and we’ll notify you as soon as your device arrives at our facility. 
3
####  Get Your Exact Offer 
Once we inspect your Mac, we’ll contact you with the final confirmed offer. Approve it and receive fast payment, or decline and have your device returned — no pressure, no hidden fees. We will send your payment using PayPal, Venmo, Cash App, or by check through the mail — whichever is most convenient for you.

## Assess Device Condition
Your quoted value is based on the information provided and confirmed upon final inspection.
View Device Inspection Tips
  * **Select "No"** if the device has issues powering on and off.  
**Select "No"** if the device has Liquid Damage.  
**Select "No"** if the device has Bad Battery.  
**Select "No"** if the device has other Power Issues.  

Does your device power on?More Info
Yes No 
  * **Select "No"** if the device has Admin or iCloud or MDM  
**Select "No"** if the device has macOS Booting Issues  
**Select "No"** if the device has other Hardware issues  

Does the device function properly?More Info
Yes No 
  * **Select "No"** if the device has Cracked or malfunctioning LCD  
**Select "No"** if the device has Cracks, dents or severe scratches to the housing, sticker marks or fading

**Select "No"** if the device has Keyboard or Trackpad or Speakers or other non-functional components

### Simple Four Point Inspection
#### Power Up + Software Check
Power up your device and check that the operating system and software operates correctly.
#### Check Screen + Camera
Scratches vs Cracks: Scratches on the screen are normal wear and tear, but cracks on the screen or camera are considered damage. If you run your fingernail across the area applying pressure and your fingernail catches, it is a crack, otherwise it's likely just a scratch.
Screen malfunction: Damaged screens may display only a single color, distorted colors, or flicker.
#### Check Buttons or Keyboard and Trackpad
Look for broken or missing keys. Check that all keys and buttons are functional and that the trackpad is responsive.
#### Check Housing
Minor scratches are considered normal wear and tear, but cracks and severe dents to the housing are considered damage.
